River Down Rice Market in Short Supply, Sales Active 198

▲Nanshi rice conditions were not very active yesterday. The River Down barge rice completely stopped at 5:00 PM. Changshu, Xixi North Japonica, and Su Tong gangs only had 10 units, which were all sold off. Prices rose by about one jiao compared to before. There is a lack of thin rice as a topping, and selling is relatively stable. There are not many reed ocean sharp rice, and prices are firm. New japonica is scarce, and the market shows a stable state. Bian Yuan's intention to sell goods is weak, and there are few supplies to meet the market.

▲Xinzha yesterday's weather was clear and sunny. There were not many thick japonica rice from Su Chang, and there was some sporadic sales. High and medium grades did not improve. Due to limited market conditions, stores are gradually raising prices, but they do not dare to buy too much. Thin rice such as Chonggu and Sisong is in short supply, and prices are shouted up by two jiao. The source of reed ocean sharp rice is sparse, and River Down and rice mills have a little inventory, so prices are increased by one and a half jiao. White yuan arrives and sells for a living. There is no rise or fall in the market. Western sources include Changshu, Liyang, Jiangyin, Qingpu, Sijing, Wangting, Luxu, etc. seventeen or eighteen numbers.

Taizhou White Rice Arrives in Shanghai for the First Time 199

Re-imported Foreign Rice Continues to Rise

There were still no transactions in spot foreign rice yesterday. Re-imported futures rose because the production area reported a rise, and even telegrams were not replied to. Sentiment is good. 400 tons of small twist were offered, and the price rose by another two cents. Foreign telegrams: Anli immediately loads small twist at 7 taels; Chen Jilong loads small twist in October at 6 taels 7 qian 6 cents; large twist in October at 6 taels 3 qian 7 cents; Tianxiang No. 1 Saigon immediately loads at 7 taels 3 qian 3 cents. This year's Taizhou early rice harvest is very good. Shanghai merchants have ordered 50,000 bags, and Ningbo merchants have also placed orders. Yesterday, the first batch of over 4,000 bags of white rice and brown rice, etc., were loaded. 1,800 bags of white rice were sold at a price of 12 yuan 45 jiao, and 1,000 bags of brown rice were sold at a price of 11 yuan 05 fen. It is said that it was handled by this street.

Flour Market Lackluster 200

Yesterday's flour market, after the opening in the morning, the market for each month generally showed a flat and weak trend. The price of foreign wheat continued to decline for two consecutive days, by four or five jiao. The near-term price in Chicago was as low as four and a half jiao, the lowest new record for foreign wheat. This situation seems to be an implication of oversupply, so sentiment is very lackluster. A few major manufacturers also reduced their holdings. The price ratio for each month fell by about one fen compared to the end of the previous month. Until the opening in the afternoon, because the factory selling had stopped and domestic merchants were slightly active, the momentum for the near and distant futures slightly stabilized. February was the first time it was opened for auction, with an opening price of 2 taels 1 qian 7 fen 7 li half, and a closing price of only 5 li. As a result, September was down by 7 li half, October was down by 1 fen, and November to January were down by 7 li half, it is said.

Wheat Futures in a Sluggish State 201

Yesterday's wheat futures market, after the opening in the morning and afternoon, the market for each month generally showed a sluggish trend, because the price of foreign wheat continued to decline for several days, by four or five jiao. Therefore, market sentiment was quite weak, because the large batch of American relief wheat had been finalized, but the prices were still not good. It can be seen that the oversupply of American wheat cannot be stabilized for a while. Furthermore, there are rumors that more than 100,000 tons of Russian wheat are also being sold off as much as possible. If this is true, the future will inevitably change. As a result, this month is down by 2 fen compared to the end of the previous month, October is down by 3 fen, November is down by 2 fen, December and January are down by 1 fen. February opened at 4 taels 2 qian 2 fen, and there was no change at the close. Spot wheat was very quiet because the factory's appetite was very quiet. There were few transactions, with Liuhe wheat opening at 3 taels 7 qian 2 fen, Yangzhou wheat at 3 taels 7 qian 3 fen, and Pinghu wheat at 3 taels 6 qian half. A total of over 900 bales were handled by Fuxin and Fufeng, it is said.

Sugar Market: Swire Sugar's Allocation Plate Slightly More Active 202

Yesterday's sugar market production area telegram: the current price of Cuban spot sugar is still 1.40625, the price of New York sugar futures is 1.32 in September, 1.30 in February, 1.34 in March next year, 1.40 in May; the price of Java spot sugar is 7.75, and the price of futures sugar in each month is 7.625, with no rise or fall compared to the previous telegram. The association's market allocation plate and Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse sand white had particularly quiet transactions, and the price was still 11 taels 7 qian half. High-quality goods are called for 11 taels 8 qian. No. 20 medium sand white is 11 taels 1 qian, and demand is also scarce. Swire car sugar has relatively active transactions, B mark is 12 taels, there are not many buyers, DY mark is 11 taels 8 qian half to 3 fen 7 li half, HX mark is 11 taels 7 qian 7 fen half, new arrivals that cannot be sold immediately are 11 taels 7 qian half, HM mark is 11 taels 4 qian half, transactions are quite active, the market is firm and lively, and the numbered plate transactions are also quiet. Zhenxianghao offered over 1,000 bags of old goods, washed white bags of coarse sand white, at a price of 11 taels 6 qian half, and the market atmosphere is also flat and not unusual, it is said.

Piece Goods Cloth Market Still Falling 203

The piece goods market is still sluggish, because the floods in various regions are becoming more serious, and it is difficult to expect future progress, so those who hold goods are eagerly seeking to sell them off, causing the market to continue to decline. Yesterday, fine cloth was the weakest among cotton cloths. Japanese factory goods fell again by about 1 qian. Brands such as Laba Tong Caiqiu have fallen to a price of 7 taels 3 qian half. Blue Flying Fish is 7 taels 7 qian half. Chinese goods are also weak, Qiqiu is 7 taels 8 qian, and Renzhong is 7 taels 6 qian half. The trend of fine twill is slightly better, because the shipping of dyed cloth is still relatively active, Songshu is 7 taels 05 fen, Blue Shuangyu is 7 taels 2 qian 7 fen half, and Yanghe is 7 taels 3 qian 7 fen half. Chinese goods, such as the Yingqiu Feixiong brands, are all around 7 taels 6 qian. Among coarse cloths, 14-pound feeding horse is the hardest, requiring 7 taels 2 qian, and there is not much spot stock. 13-pound, 11-pound, and 9-pound have all fallen. Since the anti-Japanese movement, the sales of Eastern goods have greatly decreased, coupled with the severe flooding, which has made the situation even more sluggish. Recently, there is a sense that there is no day without a fall. Yesterday, Zhigong neizi fell again by 2 li half, Sijunzi was 3 qian 05 li, Lieyan was 3 qian 5 fen 2 li half, Moganshan was 3 qian 5 fen half, fine bibiji and Huxinting were 3 qian 2 fen 7 li half, Huanle was 3 qian 2 fen half, and the rest fell uniformly. Sales were slightly active in the Sichuan gang yesterday, it is said.

Silk, Tea, and Dry Cocoon Factories Enjoy Prosperous Advances 204

▲Bottom Stock Is Thin, Supply Does Not Meet Demand: Cocoon Merchants Hoard, Prices Continue to Rise This year, the spring and summer cocoons in various regions of Jiangsu and Zhejiang have all reported poor harvests, which are not enough for reeling. The market is becoming more and more stable. Recently, because silk public bonds have been issued, various silk factories are preparing to start work and are starting to replenish raw materials. Dry cocoon factories are enjoying prosperous advances, but the bottom stock is thin, and supply does not meet demand. Cocoon merchants are hoarding, and asking prices are getting higher and higher. Currently, the market price of self-reeled cocoons must be 820 to 30 taels, which is a sharp increase of 40 to 50 taels compared to before, it is said.

Luzhuang Zhenmei Has Active Sales and Rising Prices 205

Yesterday, at the foreign tea market in Shanghai, the Zhenmei green teas from Wuyuan, Tunxi, and other regions, and the large foreign firms such as Yingzhuang Xiehe, Jinlong, Tongfu, and Dute, seeing that the market inventory was drying up and overseas demand was extremely urgent, increased prices to seek goods, and the market was unusually lively. Selling prices rose again by four or five taels. The Gongxi item is in demand by various English and Russian firms, and the market has also loosened slightly. The green tea market is showing an extremely firm trend, it is said.
